<script id="merchNapkinWorker" type="javascript/worker">
self.onmessage = function(e) {
	var request = e.data;
	if(request && request.type && request.type =="request"){
		doAjaxCall(request.url, request.timeout);
	}
};

function getXMLHttpClient(){
    var xmlhttp=null;
	try {
	    xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest();
    } catch (e) {
		var XMLHTTP_IDS = new Array('MSXML2.XMLHTTP.5.0',
		    'MSXML2.XMLHTTP.4.0',
		    'MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0',
		    'MSXML2.XMLHTTP',
		    'Microsoft.XMLHTTP' );
		for (var i=0;i < XMLHTTP_IDS.length && !success; i++) {
   			try {
        	    xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject(XMLHTTP_IDS[i]);
    	    } catch (e) {}
	    }
    }
    return xmlhttp;
}


function doAjaxCall(url, timeout){
	var xhttp = getXMLHttpClient();
	var startAjaxTimer = (new Date()).getTime()

	xhttp.onreadystatechange = function() {
		if (xhttp.readyState == 4) {
			xhttp.ontimeout = null;
			var ajaxResponseTime = ((new Date()).getTime()) - startAjaxTimer
			self.postMessage({'type':'response',
				'status': xhttp.status,
				'timeTaken': ajaxResponseTime,
				'responseText': xhttp.responseText
			});
 		}
	};

	xhttp.open("GET", url, true);
	xhttp.send('');
	xhttp.timeout = timeout;
    xhttp.ontimeout = function (e) {
    xhttp.onreadystatechange = null;
		var ajaxResponseTime = ((new Date()).getTime()) - startAjaxTimer
        self.postMessage({'type' : 'error', 'status' : 'timeout', 'timeTaken': ajaxResponseTime});
    };
}
</script>

<script>
		if(typeof window.merch == 'undefined'){
			window.merch = {};
		}

		window.merch.napkinResponseArray = [];
		window.merch.collapsePlmtArray = []
		window.merch.napkinResponseRequested=false;

		window.merch.napkinResponseHandler = function(fromRequest){
			var broadCastResponse = false;
			if(fromRequest){
				if(window.merch && window.merch.napkinResponseArray && window.merch.napkinResponseArray.length>0){
					broadCastResponse=true;
				}else{
					window.merch.napkinResponseRequested = true;
				}
			}else{
				if(window.merch.napkinResponseRequested){
					broadCastResponse=true;
				}
			}
			if(broadCastResponse){
				//Assume jquery is available by this time
				if($){
					$(document).trigger('_ADS_NAPKIN_RESPONSE');
				}
			}
		}

		window.merch.initMerchXMLHttpClient = function(){ var xmlhttp=null; try { xmlhttp = new XMLHttpRequest(); } catch (e) { var XMLHTTP_IDS = new Array('MSXML2.XMLHTTP.5.0','MSXML2.XMLHTTP.4.0','MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0','MSXML2.XMLHTTP','Microsoft.XMLHTTP' ); for (var i=0;i < XMLHTTP_IDS.length && !success; i++) { try { xmlhttp = new ActiveXObject(XMLHTTP_IDS[i]); } catch (e) {}}} return xmlhttp;}

		window.merch.collapsePlacement = function(data){
			try{
				if(!data || !data.pIds || data.pIds.length===0)
					return;

				data.pIds.forEach(function(pId){
					var div_id = 'placement_html_' + pId,
							div = document.getElementById(div_id),
							pIdIndex = window.merch.collapsePlmtArray.indexOf(pId);

					if(div){
						div.style.display = 'none';
					}

					if(!div || div.style.display != 'none'){

						if(pIdIndex == -1){
							window.merch.collapsePlmtArray = window.merch.collapsePlmtArray.concat(pId);
						}
					}else{
						if(pIdIndex > -1){
							window.merch.collapsePlmtArray.splice(pIdIndex, 1);
						}
					}
				});
			}catch(e){}
		}

		var textContent = document.querySelector('#merchNapkinWorker').textContent;
		function createMerchNapkinWorker() {
			if(typeof(Worker) !== "undefined") {
				var blob = new Blob([textContent]);
				var worker = new Worker(window.URL.createObjectURL(blob));
				return worker;
			} else {
				return undefined;
			}
		}
	</script>

	<script>
			(function (){
				var plmtIds = [101197];

				var trackingJson = window.merch.trackingJson;
				var retryCount = 0;
				var maxRetryCount = 1;
				var retryDelay = 50;

				var populateClientDataForTracking = function(status, timeTaken, additionalClientInfo) {
					var clientData = "clientStatus:" + status + "|clientTime:" + timeTaken + "|client:napkin" + '|retryCount:' + retryCount + (additionalClientInfo ? additionalClientInfo : "");

					for(var index in plmtIds) {
						var key = plmtIds[index];
						if(trackingJson[key] && trackingJson[key][0] && trackingJson[key][0].eventProperty){
							trackingJson[key][0].eventProperty.clientdata = clientData;
							window.merch.trackingJson = trackingJson;
						}
					}
				}

				function onNapkinResponseReady() {
					window.dispatchEvent(new Event('NAPKIN_RESPONSE_READY'));
					window.NAPKIN_RESPONSE_READY = true;
				}

				var napkinUrl='https://www.ebay.com/npk/napkinapi/v1/ticketing/redeem?ticket=napkin-7fba1ec0-eac6-4c4f-bad1-8fbe07531b37';
				if(napkinUrl){
					var merchNapkinWorker = createMerchNapkinWorker();

					var makeNapkinCall = function () {
						merchNapkinWorker.postMessage({
							'type' : 'request',
							'url': napkinUrl,
							'timeout': 2000
						});
					}

					var retryNapkinCall = function (response) {
						if (retryCount < maxRetryCount) {
							retryCount = retryCount + 1;
							setTimeout(makeNapkinCall, retryDelay * retryCount);
						} else {
							populateClientDataForTracking(response.status, response.timeTaken, '|error:failed');
							window.merch.collapsePlacement({pIds:plmtIds});
							onNapkinResponseReady();
						}
					}

					merchNapkinWorker.onmessage = function(e) {
						var response = e.data;
						if(response && response.type === "response") {
							if (response.status === 200) {
								if(window.merch && window.merch.napkinResponseArray){
									populateClientDataForTracking(response.status, response.timeTaken);
									window.merch.napkinResponseArray.push({pIds:plmtIds, responseText:response.responseText});
									window.merch.napkinResponseHandler(false);
									onNapkinResponseReady();
								}
							} else {
								retryNapkinCall(response);
							}
						} else if (response && response.type === "error") {
							if (response.status === "timeout") {
								retryNapkinCall(response);
							}
						}
					};

					if(merchNapkinWorker) {
						makeNapkinCall();
					} else {
						populateClientDataForTracking("UnsupportedWebWorker", -1, '|error:failed');
						window.merch.collapsePlacement({pIds:plmtIds});
						onNapkinResponseReady();
					}

				}
			})();
		</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
        var _plsUBTTQ = [];
        var _plsubtInp = {"eventFamily": "ITM", "samplingRate": 100, "disableImp": true, "pageId": 2047675, "app": "viewitem"};
        function addPulsarEvent(event) { _plsUBTTQ.push(event); }
        function getPulsarEvents() { return _plsUBTTQ; }

        // On window load, check to see if PulsarUBT.js is already on the page somewhere
        // if not, create a script element and load it ourselves.
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            var pulsarScriptSrc = "https://ir.ebaystatic.com/rs/v/s0hteylevy4bpkd12dvkd4yi5ms.js";
            var pulsarScriptTagExists = isResourceAlreadyAttached(pulsarScriptSrc, "script", "src");

            if (!pulsarScriptTagExists) {
                var scriptTag = document.createElement("script");
                scriptTag.setAttribute("type", "text/javascript");
                scriptTag.setAttribute("src", pulsarScriptSrc);
                document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0].appendChild(scriptTag);
            }
        });

        function isResourceAlreadyAttached(url,tagType, attribute) {
            if (!url)
                return;

            var resources = document.getElementsByTagName(tagType);
            for (var i = resources.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
                if (resources[i][attribute] === url)
                    return true;
            }
            return false;
        }
    </script>
    <script type="text/javascript">
        function handleDisabledCTATracking(e) {
            var disabledCTA = e.target.querySelector('.ux-call-to-action');
            var disabledCTAIdentifier = disabledCTA && disabledCTA.getAttribute('data-track-disabled');
            var trackingId = '152606';

            if (disabledCTAIdentifier) {
                var trackingObj = {
                    'eventFamily': 'ITM',
                    'eventAction': 'ACTN',
                    'actionKind': 'CLICK',
                    'flushImmediately': false,
                    'eventProperty': {
                        'disabledCTA': disabledCTAIdentifier,
                        'moduledtl': 'li:' + trackingId,
                        'sid': 'l' + trackingId
                    }
                }

                // Porting over and hardcoding the format and trigger logic from the tracking-util in Node
                var eventType = 'customEvts'; //eventType should be hard coded as customEvts according to Pulsar docs
                var eventFamily = trackingObj.eventFamily;
                var eventAction = trackingObj.eventAction;
                var eventAttributes = Object.assign({}, {'flushImmediately': trackingObj.flushImmediately}, trackingObj.eventProperty);

                if (window && window.addPulsarEvent) {
                    window.addPulsarEvent([eventType, eventFamily, eventAction, eventAttributes]);
                }
            }
        }

        window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', (event) => {
            document.querySelectorAll('[data-track-disabled]').forEach(function(item) {
                if (item.parentElement) {
                    item.parentElement.addEventListener('click', handleDisabledCTATracking);
                }
            });
        });
    </script>
